Wang Qingquan, a Kidnapping Victim, Escapes After a Month

Shaoxing Bandits Threaten

Shave Beard, Change Clothes, Move to Chongming

Wine and Delicacies, Dead Drunk

Jump Out of Window, Flee to Police Station

Wang Qingquan, a broker at the Shanghai Gauze Exchange, 52 years old, was kidnapped by bandits on January 6th of this year at around 8:00 AM while riding in his private car to the exchange. The incident occurred near Wang Xinyi Ham outside Xiaonanmen. For several months, there has been no news, and rumors outside said that the bandits had already killed him. Now, after inquiries from various sources, it is learned that Wang is still alive and has escaped. After Wang was kidnapped by the bandits, he was imprisoned in a remote bandit lair in a certain village. His beard was forcibly shaved off by the bandits, and his clothes were changed to avoid attention. Later, with the outbreak of the Shanghai war, the bandits transferred him to a sailboat and sailed to a sandbar about two miles east of the Chongming Siji. The surveillance was quite strict, and a small boat came every day to deliver news. All the bandits were from Shaoxing, and they often threatened Wang. Because Wang was old and sick, he had long disregarded life and death, so he closed his eyes and did not answer. Because the bandits had been there for a long time and observed that Wang was old and weak, the surveillance became slightly lax. The other day, the bandits suddenly bought fine wine and delicacies, and they ate and drank heavily. Before long, they were dead drunk. Wang saw such a good opportunity and jumped out of the window without waiting. He set foot on the sand and ran a mile away. He met a villager on the way, who directed him to the Chongming County Fourth District Public Office, where he reported the situation. The District Chief, Xu Dechang, immediately ordered the police to rush to arrest the bandits, but the bandits had already fled, so they were not found. Because Wang had been in the bandit's lair for too long and his nerves were stimulated, resulting in erratic behavior, he was sent to the Third Hospital in the area for recuperation. At the same time, his family was notified to come and claim him.

A Disturbance Over a Dressmaker's Dress

Li Huizhen Eager to Try on New Clothes

Chen Fushan Invited to "Have Tea" and Explain

Li Huizhen, a woman from Suzhou, in her early twenties, works as a dancer. She lives at No. 25 Yongnian Lane, Baker Road. On the 20th of this month, the Saint Anna Dance Hall, newly opened on the site of the old Paris Dance Hall opposite the Zhaofeng Garden in West Shanghai, Li began working there as a dancer. Because she was new, her clothing had to be beautiful and fashionable. Therefore, on the 20th, she specially selected white serge fabric and brought it to the Xieshun Chinese and Western Clothing Store opened by Chen Fushan at No. 4 Cian Lane, Tianjin Road, instructing him to make a Western-style short coat with black edges. Because she was eager to wear it, she needed to pick it up the next day. Chen replied that it would take a week to make, but if it was for temporary wear, she could pick it up the next day. Therefore, he rushed to finish it overnight. When she sent someone to pick up the short coat on the 21st, she returned it on the 22nd, saying that the style was not good and asked him to quickly modify it. After the modification, she was still not satisfied. At that time, there was a verbal conflict, and they immediately started fighting. The shop owner, Chen Fushan's finger was bitten by Li, and the counter was overturned. The beaded bracelet on Li's arm also fell to the ground and broke, and two small beads were lost. Later, the Chinese police arrived and took both parties to the police station. The chief thought it was a trivial matter and did not handle it, and warned both parties not to argue again in the future. But on the morning of the day before yesterday, a Ningbo man, Zhang Chunhe, suddenly came to Chen Fushan's place and invited Chen to have tea at the Leyuan Tea House on Jiujiang Road to reason. Chen, fearing something unexpected, secretly reported to the Laozha Police Station, who sent detectives Li Xiushan and Sun Dafa to pretend to be tea customers and wait. Chen, accompanied by his relative Zhu Yinbo, went to the tea house. There, he saw that Li Huizhen had already arrived with Zhang Chunhe, Pan Defa, Ye Xiangshun, and Ding Zhaojin, sitting at the same table. Zhang stepped forward and started to negotiate with Chen, and the others echoed, creating a menacing atmosphere, saying that if he didn't cooperate, there would be trouble. As a result, they agreed on 30 yuan. Chen paid 15 yuan first, and the remaining half was sent to No. 159 Hankou Road according to Zhang's note. At that time, the detectives immediately stepped forward and arrested Li Huizhen and the other five people, and took the cash to the police station, where they were detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the Special District. According to the police lawyer Ru Baoyi, he prosecuted the defendants for extortion under Article 370 of the Criminal Law and detailed the case, requesting severe punishment for the second defendant, Zhang Chunhe, because Zhang was the leader of the case and took advantage of people's disputes to carry out his extortion and profit from it. The victim, Chen Fushan, also borrowed Zhu Yinbo's testimony to the court, explaining the situation. When questioned, Li Huizhen confessed that Chen had made the clothes badly and had beaten her, breaking the beaded bracelet, so she demanded compensation for the loss. Zhang Chunhe admitted that he was entrusted by Li to demand 18 yuan from Chen for the cost of the fabric and 12 yuan for the two beads. The other three, Pan Defa, etc., all denied their involvement. They hired four lawyers, Fan Gang, Yang Linzhi, etc., to defend them. After the court president Qian Hongye verified the confessions, he sentenced all the defendants to joint extortion. Zhang Chunhe was sentenced to six months of imprisonment and a fine of 30 yuan. Li Huizhen, Pan Defa, Ye Xiangshun, and Ding Zhaojin were each fined 30 yuan. Li Huizhen's sentence was suspended for three years.

Northern Shanghai Gambling Dens Under Japanese Protection

Report from the Anti-Opium Association

The Chinese National Anti-Opium Association issued a report yesterday on the investigation of the opening of opium in Northern Shanghai, stating that after the outbreak of the Shanghai Incident, after the Japanese army occupied the area near the concession, the Northern Shanghai Local Maintenance Association was established by Japanese-instigated Chinese traitors in the area around Tiantong Road, Wuhua Road, and Linping Road near Dithmarschen Road in Hongkou. All political power fell into the hands of the Japanese. In the past month, within a two-square-mile radius of this area, opium dens and gambling houses have been set up one after another under the protection of the Japanese. City signs are widely posted, and business is open. Once you enter the area, it is like being in a foreign country. Initially, it was tentatively agreed to collect a fee of 300 yuan per day. In the past three weeks, business has been booming, and the total donation from gambling houses has increased to 1,200 yuan per day. There are about 500 opium pipes, and each pipe is taxed two jiao per day, totaling about 100 yuan per day. All of this is collected daily by the Maintenance Association and handed over to the Japanese. Such a huge sum is truly shocking to hear. The license numbers and addresses of each gambling house and opium den are listed below: Shunli Company, No. 4 Jishan Lane, Tiantong Road; Jiufu Company Clubhouse, No. 2 Lane, Shande Lane, Tiantong Road; Defa Company, No. 9 Jishan Lane, Tiantong Road; Dafa Company Flower Association Reception Office, at the back door of the same address; Hongli Clubhouse, Nos. 38-40 Renxin Lane, Hongzhen; Hongjin Clubhouse, Nos. 50-52 Lizhong Lane, Hongzhen; Fuli Company Clubhouse, Sande Lane, Wuhua Road; Fuli Branch, No. 107 Derun Road; Fuli Company, No. 146 Linping Road; Shengli Company, No. 4 Shangde Lane, Shengji Road; Qiaji Company, No. 156 Linping Road; Hongchanghao, No. 19 Tiande Lane, Wuhua Road; Xiechengchang, No. 88 Derun Road; Woyunxuan, No. 4 Yiyi Lane, Tiantong Road; Anlegong, No. 9 Jishan Lane, Tiantong Road; Heli Company, No. 118 Tiantong Road, upstairs of Yongyuxiang Metal Shop; Sanxingshe, No. 66 Derun Road, upstairs of Zhu Mingyang's Lecture Hall; Rongjishe, No. 90 Linping Road; Xinxin Branch, No. 99 Derun Road; Xiaoyao Xuan, No. 3 Wuhua Lane, Wuhua Road; Sanxing Company, No. 2 Lane, Xinhua Lane, Tianbao Road; Zhongxingshe, No. 99 Tiandou Road; Tiansheshe, No. 142 Linping Road; Risheshe, No. 148 Linping Road; Jiushun Company, inside Qingshan Lane, Wuhua Road. The larger opium and gambling companies, such as Jiufu, Shunli, and Fuli, have brightly lit doors, are full of customers, and have plenty of staff and attentive service. Red strips with the words "Welcome to Visit" are posted outside. Other places either sell "Su cigarettes" or red tonic pills (i.e., red pills). The quiet streets of the past have suddenly become bustling scenes. The related social situations have undergone the following changes: (1) Good households are moving away because they cannot bear the filth; (2) Tea houses, dim sum shops, and soda stalls are increasing; (3) Rent is four times higher than before; (4) Cars and rickshaws with opium smokers have increased twentyfold; (5) Waiters are all over the streets, like...It is said that on the 24th, two gambling customers were shot and killed by the Hongli and Shunli companies for robbing gambling customers of over 700 yuan in profits. The Japanese arrested the accounting staff of the two companies, causing a great disturbance.

Educational News Highlights

Ministry of Education Improves Universities and Colleges in Peiping

Nanjing, 25th (Telegraph) - The Ministry of Education believes that there is overlap in the departments of universities and colleges in Peiping. It is appropriate to comprehensively consider and plan, and according to the principle of division of labor and cooperation, each school should be able to concentrate its efforts to engage in special improvements and development. A special order was issued to the presidents and deans of each school to hold a meeting to discuss, and Jiang Menglin and Shen Yinmo will schedule a meeting.

Local

Municipal Education Bureau Announces Regulations for Guest Students in Secondary Schools

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday ordered the city's municipal and private secondary schools, saying: "After investigating the city since the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War, schools in Zhabei and Jiangwan have been unable to start school as scheduled or have temporarily suspended operations due to the war. As a result, many students have transferred to other places or are guest students in other schools. Various secondary schools in the city have therefore recruited guest students, and there are occasional cases of arbitrary enrollment without any investigation, which can easily lead to abuses. In order to refer to the current situation of various guest student schools, the Shanghai Municipal Secondary School Guest Student Regulations have been drafted and presented to the Ministry of Education and the government for instructions. Approval has been granted for filing. The Shanghai Municipal Secondary School Guest Student Regulations are copied and sent to your school for compliance. Please be informed." Attached is a copy of the Shanghai Municipal Secondary School Guest Student Regulations: (1) Students whose schools are unable to start school as scheduled or have temporarily suspended operations due to the war, and have been approved by the Bureau, may temporarily be guest students in other schools. (2) Students of public or registered private schools should be guest students in public or registered private schools. (3) Students of unregistered private schools who are guest students in public or registered private schools shall not be issued transfer certificates by the guest student schools. (4) Students of unregistered private schools who are guest students in public or registered private schools, when the guest student schools issue grade reports, should indicate the name of the student's original school. (5) The term of guest students is limited to one semester. (6) Schools that have temporarily suspended operations and whose students are guest students in other schools should report the details of the contact with the guest student schools, along with a list of guest students to the Bureau (the list should include name, guest student school, place of origin, age, department and grade of the original school, department and grade of the transferred school, the amount of tuition fees paid, and remarks). (7) At the end of the semester, the guest student schools should transfer the grades of the guest students to the original schools for submission to the Bureau for record. The original schools will then report the grades to the students' families. (8) Guest students in the first and second grades who pass the exam may have the guest student schools issue a certificate of completion for the semester, and the certificate must indicate the name of the original school. (9) Guest students in the final grade who have passed the required credits and examinations should transfer to the original school. If the original school believes that they have completed their studies and met the time limit, the original school may issue a diploma. (10) Diplomas issued should be sent to the Bureau for verification, along with various forms. The issuance of diplomas should be handled in accordance with the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's regulations on student graduation. (11) Guest students in the first and second grades who wish to become regular students should follow the transfer procedures of the respective schools. (12) These regulations will be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Minutes of the County Education Bureau's Bureau Affairs Meeting

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 242nd Bureau Affairs Meeting yesterday morning. Those present were Director Shi, Zheng Guozhai, Yang Huimin, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, Qian Zhonghou, Shen Jingzhi, Zheng Shaoyuan, Yan Chongguang, and Xi Siwu. Director Shi presided over the meeting, and Pan Shengshan took the minutes. After the usual formalities, the reported matters were omitted. It was resolved that it was difficult to approve due to the regulations of the Provincial Department. Record of Striking the Bell at the Ancient Temple (6): The Unswept Courtyard and the Studious Husband

In the middle of the night, a violent and urgent knocking on the door jolted me awake. This was followed by the sounds of commotion, cold laughter, and shouts of fighting from the village. I put on my clothes, opened the door, and saw that it was none other than the monk's godson, A-Yang. He was out of breath from running, and told me, in a panic, "Father has been tied up. Please go and plead for him."

I hurriedly locked the temple gate and followed A-Yang, running towards the village to save the monk. Several torches were lit in front of A-Yang's house. As I approached the gate, I heard people shouting, "Take them to the city! ...That would be a sight to see! ...Zhong'er is here! Good, Zhong'er! Go in and see what your great monk has been up to." Two stark naked people were tied together in a heap! One was A-Yang's wet nurse, and the other was the monk. A rural scene of catching adulterers was unfolding before my eyes.

When the monk saw me, he said, "Good Zhong'er! Please, beg them to release me." I took off my short coat and covered them, saying, "I am willing to plead on your behalf." Could I refuse the monk's request? No, absolutely not. I said to the villagers, "Let them stay here for a moment, and we'll go to the teahouse to talk."

"Talk, and see if there is any solution," suggested the blacksmith, Old Li. He suggested sending two people to stand guard here. Everyone agreed, and we went to the teahouse to begin negotiations.

I asked, "What do you plan to do?"

Everyone said, "Send them to the county!"

I asked, "Was the monk's action rape?"

Everyone said, "They've been an old couple for years! Don't you know how much they love each other!"

I asked, "Does A-Yang's mother have a husband? How old is she this year?"

The blacksmith, Old Li, said, "A-Yang's mother is a pitiful woman. She lost her husband at twenty-two, and is now twenty-five years old."

I said, "Lawyer Zhao Gongping once came to the temple to visit. I asked him many legal questions, and he said that if an unmarried man and an unmarried woman over twenty years old are willing to be together, it is not against the law. In that case, even if you send the monk to the county, the county will certainly not be able to convict him. In the end, you will only waste your energy and money."

The carpenter, Old Wu, said, "Who wants to meddle in such affairs? This is all caused by someone being jealous!"

I said, "We must always think ahead and consider the consequences before we act. We cannot act rashly."

Everyone said, "In your opinion, what should be done about this matter?"

I said, "According to Buddhist rules, if you are a monk, you are not allowed to marry. If you want to marry, you cannot be a monk. Since he wants a wife, he should no longer be a monk. We can start a school in the temple so that all the children in the village can attend. If he is willing, we can allocate ten acres of land to the couple, only for their own cultivation and consumption, not to be mortgaged or sold to others. In the future, they can become self-sufficient people in the village. If everyone agrees, I will go and talk to him."

Everyone deliberated for some time, and in the end, except for the jealous bricklayer, Old Xu, everyone agreed that my plan was a win-win situation.

The monk was more than willing. Old Li untied their ropes, and this romantic affair was resolved. Later, after he officially married A-Yang's mother, I went to his wedding feast. He thanked me especially and invited me to sit in the seat of honor.

An enemy turned into a friend, an ancient temple became a school—all of this happened in a matter of hours. How incredible!

Shanghai Education After January 28th (11): Still

Seventeen. Make-up Lessons During the Holidays

Originally, middle schools should have started classes on February 4th, and elementary schools on February 3rd. Summer vacation was to begin on June 29th for middle schools and July 1st for elementary schools. The school calendar stipulated that the first semester would have 142 days of classes for middle schools and 145 days for elementary schools. This was according to the regulations for the 20th year, and it should not be changed arbitrarily. In the past, when schools took unauthorized holidays or teachers missed classes, it was considered a national crisis. However, this spring in Shanghai, the situation was pressing. It was fortunate enough that schools could barely open, a truly auspicious and congratulatory event. Nevertheless, the missed classes should be made up in order to fulfill the responsibility of nurturing people and saving the nation. Therefore, the Municipal Education Bureau drafted a "Measures for Reducing Holidays and Making Up Classes in Primary and Secondary Schools This Semester," ordering all schools to comply and submit their opening dates and make-up schedules for review. The measures for emphasizing education and making up classes during the holidays are listed for reference below:

1. Schools that started classes before February 15th must follow the school calendar for the summer vacation.

2. Schools that started classes after February 15th but before February 29th should shorten the summer vacation by two weeks according to the school calendar.

3. Schools that started classes after February 29th but before March 15th should shorten the summer vacation by three weeks according to the school calendar.

4. Schools that started classes after March 15th but before March 31st should teach until the end of the semester.

Of the Shang Gong Elementary School

A Corner of the Science Museum of National Jinan University Bombed

(Photo by Ye Changlie)

5. Schools that start classes in April will not have a summer vacation, but graduating students must finish early.

6. Spring break for this semester is completely canceled.

7. If schools suspend classes after opening, they should make up for them during holidays.

8. All schools should report their opening and holiday dates, as well as any suspensions and make-up plans, to this bureau for record.

The reporter made a rough calculation: almost no schools need to make up classes completely, but a very few do; those that need to make up classes for the entire summer vacation account for 5%; those that postpone the summer vacation by two weeks account for 58%; and those that make up classes for half of the summer vacation account for about 36%. It seems that when the sun is scorching and the weather is hot and humid, schools in Shanghai will have to work like farmers in the fields.

On the 19th, the second research meeting will be held at the High School Department of Shanghai Provincial Shanghai Middle School, Lujiabang, Xiaonanmen, Shanghai, to discuss "Teaching Methods for Elementary School Work Subjects" and "Guidance Issues." You are requested to send a representative to the meeting and to submit proposals to Mr. Lu Shaoji, Normal Department of Shanghai Middle School, before June 10th for advance preparation. Thank you very much.

Maolai Breaks Our Country's Javelin Record

The Outstanding Feature of the U.S. Soldier McKinley's Track and Field Performance

Is That They Are All Close to Our Country's Highest Records

The Six Giants Sports Meet will be held at the beginning of next month. In order to examine the results, McKinley, a U.S. soldier stationed in Shanghai, held a joint sports meet for various battalions at the Zhonghua Track and Field Field at 9 a.m. on the 24th. The Third Battalion continued to hold the championship, scoring 64 points. The runner-up was the First Battalion with 56 points, and the Headquarters finished last with 18 points. Now, let's look at the following results:

Schwank Wins the Championship

Schwank of the Third Battalion not only had outstanding results, but also won the individual championship, winning three first places and breaking two records, for a total of 15 points. The second individual was "Little Treasure" Sutton, a famous middle-distance runner, who won first place in both the 1600 meters and 800 meters. The famous short-distance runner Tang Sly, who is well-known on the sea, was defeated by Alate in the 200 meters, and tied with Digge for third individual.

China's Javelin Record

Officer Maolai, short and stout, with extraordinary coordination, was already well-known in the Shanghai track and field scene last year. In this javelin competition, Maolai suddenly created an amazing performance, with a score of 156 feet 2 inches. The score of the second place, Fileno, also reached 150 feet 9 inches. Not only is it a new Shanghai record, but also a new national record for our country. The highest record in our country was created by Wen Dingxin with 45.90 meters, which is only 150 feet 6 feet 6 inches in English feet.

Two Heroes Compete in the Sprinting World

Shi Tanglai, who has been famous for a long time, swept all the first places from 100 meters to 400 meters in the International Sports Meet in Shanghai last year. However, this time, he was defeated by Roger-style football star Alate in the 200 meters. Ah's score was 24.2 seconds. The 100-meter race was still won by Shi. Alate started extremely fast, obviously faster than Shi, but Alate looked back at others while running, which reduced his speed and allowed Shi Tanglai to win the championship with a time of 11.4 seconds.

Schwank's Three Masterpieces

Schwank is also famous in the track and field world. On this day, he won the first place in the pole vault, long jump, and triple jump. The pole vault also set a new Shanghai record with a score of 11 feet 1 inch, breaking his own previous best score of 11 feet and a quarter of an inch. Although it is still not as good as Fu Baolu's 11 feet 7 inches (3.54 meters) in our country, it is feared that our country's athletes will hardly be able to reach it at present. Also, Shi's long jump was 19 feet 8 inches, and the triple jump was 39 feet 5 inches.

Characteristics of Discus and Shot Put

In addition, Beck's 16-pound shot put, with a score of 42 feet 9 inches, is also not as good as the highest record in our country. Digge's discus was 111 feet 7 inches, which is very close to Zhang Lingjia's 34.63 meters (113 feet 7 feet) in our country and the 35.40 meters used by Lian Zeng last year (116 feet 7 inches).

The Rest of the Results Are Average

The high and low are all average, and there is not much to introduce. Brown's 400 meters was 55.2 seconds, and Grove's high jump was 5 feet 2 inches 4 points and 3, Sutton's 800 meters was 2 minutes 12.2 seconds, which is not weak. Also, Sutton's 1600 meters was 5 minutes 7 sand 8.

Our Country's Athletes Should Also Be Careful

In the Six Giants Sports Meet to be held on the 4th of next month, McKinley will hold his highest authority. Although the Zhongqing side has already recruited the best players in Shanghai, it is still feared that it is not optimistic. In the jumping department, except for the pole vault, our country can have hope. The first place in the throwing department is feared not to be ours. The situation in the track events is equal. In short, McKinley is a strong enemy of Zhongqing, and we must be prepared to defend against him.

Free Talk

The Old Noodle Shop Owner's Record of Sharpening His Sword

— Gu Mingdao

The old noodle shop owner's surname is unknown. Let us call him by this name for now. The old man has been running his shop in Goubangzi for more than ten years. He is as industrious as the one in Jinzhou and is full of vigor. After the September 18th Incident, the Japanese bandits took over and their iron hooves ravaged the Liaoning Province. Only Jinzhou was still in our hands. However, the Japanese army coveted it very much and would not allow our Northeast Army to have a foothold there. Therefore, they transferred troops westward. The Japanese were eager to try. Goubangzi happened to be in the path of their advance. The people fled to the interior of the Guanzhong area. The old man gave all his assets to his son and daughter-in-law, urging them to leave quickly. But he remained alone. His son and daughter-in-law pleaded with him strongly, but could not persuade him. They left with tears in their eyes. The old man was not afraid at all and opened his shop as usual. He said to people in between, "The Japanese bandits are like greedy snakes, recommended to eat our country. Those who guard the land cannot fulfill their responsibilities. They are eager for internal wars and cowardly in resisting foreign enemies. They are lending weapons to the enemy and providing food to the thieves. They are sitting idly by and watching the enemy's cavalry invade the west without being able to resist. This is abandoning the people of our Eastern Province to the mouths of tigers and wolves. What could be more heartbreaking than this? I am old. When the country is in trouble, why should I avoid it? If the Japanese bandits come, I will find a way to harm them." Before long, the proposal for a neutral zone in Jinzhou failed. The Japanese army entered from Changfu as expected. Goubangzi fell in no time. After the Japanese army arrived, the old man opened his shop as usual, and even smoked his pipe, remaining exceptionally calm. Four or five Japanese soldiers entered his shop. Seeing him, they laughed and said, "This old man is much bolder than the young ones. Are you willing to be a docile subject of our great Japan? We will protect you and not kill you." The old man said yes, yes. The Japanese soldiers first ordered the old man to taste the noodles he made. The old man immediately put down his pipe and began to make noodles. He served them in a large bowl and presented them to the Japanese soldiers. The Japanese soldiers first ordered the old man to taste them to test if they were poisoned. The old man calmly finished a bowl first. He said to the Japanese soldiers, "Why are you so timid? Who would poison people?" The Japanese soldiers laughed and then ate with peace of mind. But in less than an hour, the poison took effect. They cried out in pain and fell to the ground one after another. The old man also suffered severe pain and could not hold on. He collapsed in the shop. It turned out that the old man had put a lot of arsenic in the noodles when he made them, hoping to poison the Japanese soldiers to death. The reason why he willingly tasted them first was that he had already resolved to die. If he did not do so, it would not be enough to make the cunning Japanese soldiers die with him. Mr. Zhu Aoyun served in Huangguantun. He fled to Shanghai from Ping after the looting. He recounted this matter to me. The sage said, "The brave are fearless." Such an old man is probably in the stream of the brave. He is worthy to be compared with the young French girl in Mei Village, who designed to deceive the enemy. This echoes across ancient and modern times.

A Wounded Soldier in the 19th Army

— Zheng

The Japanese army has retreated. The day before yesterday, I went to my hometown of Nanxiang alone and saw many compatriots who had suffered. They were supporting the old and carrying the young, with bitter smiles on their faces, returning to their long-separated homes one after another. The trenches along the way were still facing each other. At noon, I finally entered the town. The scene of desolation was touching and made people shed tears. Upon arriving home, a gatekeeper named Abiao recounted an inhumane act committed by a Japanese soldier. Therefore, I record it below.

When the loyal and brave 19th Route Army swiftly retreated to the second line of defense, a rear hospital inside a certain ancestral hall had to be moved to Kunsu in a very short time. Therefore, the wounded soldiers were hurriedly carried away. But it was at night, and one soldier was lying in the rice straw and was not transported away in time. When he woke up the next morning, the Japanese army had already arrived. Upon seeing the wounded soldier, they immediately tied his hands behind his back with iron wire, causing the flesh to break and bleed. They then wrapped a long iron wire around his neck and hung him under a stone archway. Two Japanese soldiers stood to the left and right, pushing him back and forth, hitting the stone pillars of the archway. Our loyal and brave wounded soldier, speaking in Cantonese, scolded them, "You are uneducated. You are truly barbarians. I am already injured. You should not insult me like this." His voice was strong and contained no sounds of crying or begging for mercy. The two Japanese soldiers became even more angry and stabbed him more than ten times. Blood gushed out from the wounded soldier, but he still did not shout in pain. Instead, he shouted loudly, "Long live the Republic of China!" At that time, Abiao was hiding behind a tree on the opposite bank of a small river, watching from afar, but was unable to help. He only saw the withered yellow leaves under the wounded soldier stained red. The two Japanese soldiers laughed and spoke, using their rifle butts to beat him for about half an hour. Later, he heard the cries gradually weakening, sobbing more than ten times, and suddenly shouting "Long live the Republic of China!" before he died. Alas, how heroic! This wounded soldier is a pity that very few know about. Therefore, I record it to tell the people of the country.

The Philosophy of Love

— Hong Honglie

What exactly is love? It is simply an abstract term that encompasses the combined physical and spiritual interactions between human males and females, resulting in mutual affection.

To answer this question, we must study the human desire to survive and the fundamental question of what makes a person human. We know that a person is composed of both spirit and flesh, and that there is a distinction between males and females. It is through the union of males and females that humanity as a whole is formed, and that humanity can collectively organize a society of survival in the world. The greatest elements of survival are mostly two kinds: one is material needs, and the other is spiritual needs. The former belongs to carnal desires, which are the physical needs of the five senses, four limbs, and sexual organs. The latter belongs to spiritual desires, which are the mental comforts of sight, sound, smell, taste, and music. To go a step further, the former is natural, substantial, and easily seen, while the latter is hidden, imaginary, suggestive, and artistic.

These two elements have an inseparable and close relationship with life. Humans need them to harmonize his and her lives with each other, and the so-called "sexual" issue is between the flesh and the spirit.

From the perspectives of physiology, psychology, and aesthetics, men and women each possess different natural physical beauty endowed by nature. Artists study the beauty of the human body, with landscapes of high mountains, small hills, forests, and secluded valleys, and scenery of sunset, dawn, white snow, and flowers. In men, there is the magnificence of strength and majesty; in women, there are the gentleness of winding curves, the beauty of melodious and clear music, and the charm of intoxicating and soul-stirring fragrances. Therefore, men and women each have a soul that is naturally drawn to the other, and so they love and pursue each other, until the physical contact satisfies the pleasure of the spirit.

Because the Creator wants to prolong or continue the existence of humanity, there is the union of the two sexes, male and female. This kind of union is not limited to knowledge and learning, but is achievable by all things in the world—birds, fish, beasts, insects, and even grass, trees, and rocks. This is the most meaningful fundamental issue of human and all living things' survival. By understanding this fundamental principle, the issue of love can be easily solved.

Record of the Prosperity and Decline of Two Trees

— Zheng Yimei

In Jixian Nunnery near Datong Bridge in Wapu, there are two ancient ginkgo trees, each several dozen spans around. They are relics of thousands of years. One summer, there was a great wind and rain, and an ancient ginkgo tree broke off a branch, almost the size of a hug, and several feet long. But looking up at it, it only removed some of the immature branches, slightly revealing the light of the sky. Fifty miles away, in the kitchen of a certain surname in Nanxiang, there was something rising about a foot high, which could be rested on. Some say that it is the obliquely emerging root of the ancient ginkgo tree. It can be seen how large this tree is. Last year, a certain person came to the nunnery to rest. He then took out a cigarette and lit it with the remaining incense embers from the front of the Buddha shrine. He threw the incense ashes into the crevices of the ancient ginkgo tree. The tree had cracked after many years, and could hold objects. Unexpectedly, the wind blew fallen leaves, which accumulated in the crevices. Moreover, the weather was dry and arid. The fire from the burning incense ignited the leaves. The flames spread like the tongues of spirits, reaching between the trunk moss and branches. Although villagers poured water to extinguish it, a patch of it was charred black, and it no longer had its former lush and verdant appearance. Everyone thought that it was withering, and were not very sorry. Unexpectedly, this spring, the tree suddenly sprouted new branches in anger. The dense leaves covered the sun. Japanese soldiers came to invade. The villages and farmlands were all shrouded in flames, but the ancient ginkgo tree was still preserved unharmed, as if protected by spirits. This is also strange. A person who had fled from Kunshan to avoid the disaster told me this.

So, he moved a white pine from another place and transplanted it into the villa. He left a square zhang (unit of measurement) of old soil around the roots of the pine tree, fearing that the roots and the old soil would separate, or easily wither. He surrounded the square zhang of soil with cloth, wrapped it with rope, and supported it with a bamboo-woven basket. He transported it with a light carriage. When turning to go to the villa, he had to pass through a certain street.

International Debt Default (Part 1)

— Kai Xu

Everyone knows how to default on debt. The skills vary. People who live in Shanghai owe rent, and the landlord wants them to move out. They owe electricity bills, and the company wants to cut the lines. But I have heard that some people owe rent for five or six months, and the landlord does not force them to move out. They owe electricity bills for three or four months, and the company does not cut the lines. We do not investigate the details and do not know how they default on their debts. We think it is brilliant. But if you are willing to humbly ask for advice, they will happily tell you the twists and turns. Then you will suddenly understand and increase your ordinary social knowledge. Individuals have ways to default on debts, and countries also have ways to default on debts. When a person defaults on someone else's debt, it must eventually be resolved by law. As a result, they are pursued for old debts, their reputation is damaged, their credit is lost, and they cannot stand in society. But international debt default only requires getting away with it and being able to say it. The law is ineffective, and treaties are just empty words. If you have military power, you can come and fight. If I can beat you, I will fight you. If I can't beat you, I will slowly think of ways to repay the debt. If I beat you, not only will I not owe you anything, but you will have to repay me double. Because international debts are not necessarily commercial or economic loans. Many are compulsory debts. For example, after the Allied Powers won the Central Powers in the war, all the expenses of the four years of the war were lumped together and Germany was made to pay. At that time, Germany was subservient and had no choice. Saying one was one, and saying two was two. Now it's better. It has gradually risen, and it can also talk eloquently at European conferences, arguing that Germany should not bear the responsibility for the European war alone, and that Germany's domestic situation is extremely difficult and it cannot continue to repay war debts, etc. This kind of debt default is still reasonable. Germany used to be bullied, but now it refuses to continue to be a victim. So it wants to straighten its back and say a few harsh words. Now the method of defaulting on debts is even more strange. The French want to default on debts to the Americans. During the European war, France borrowed money from the United States. The United States treated France as a poor country, and was lenient with interest rates, etc. France used this money to win the war. Not only did it defeat Germany, but it also became the richest country in the world, collecting money from all over the world and depositing it in the French National Bank, causing the world's prices to rise day by day. However, it not only does not want to move its war debts to the United States, but also wants to default on them. Not only does it want to default on them, but it also bites back, saying that the United States owes France money. Not only does it say that the United States owes France money, but it also says that the United States owes money to Italy and other countries. It even wants to unite a group of debtors to make things difficult for the creditor. Do you think this kind of default is not a major international debt default? But how exactly does France default on its debts?

There was a narrow alley that could not be passed through. So, they demolished the houses and rebuilt them after the carriages passed. They valued this grand Fir so much. Since the grand Fir was planted by Shu Zhu, he held a banquet for his guests and asked them to write poems in its honor. So, the grand Fir became famous for a time. All the tourists from all over the world considered it an honor to see the grand Fir. My colleague, Mr. Jiang Xiwei, recently came from Nantong and said that the grand Fir withered and turned yellow on the day after Mr. Yu died. Now it is withered and dead, and there is no trace of any branches or remaining trunks.

Record of Military Life in Twin Buildings (63)

— Owner of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter 8: Boundless Grief in Repentance, Difficult to Achieve Optimism; Extreme Singing and Dancing for Pleasure, Glimpse of Majesty

Liang Xiaoyun asked with a smile, "How can you be sure that it will be a joke?" An Yutian was so anxious that he could only reach out to wipe the sweat from his forehead and said, "How much ability do I have? Don't you know? Moving some books around to write and fiddle with might be okay. Asking me to recruit bandits, organize militias, and establish a new army is just talking on paper. There's not even a shadow of it. If I could really rally these people, my family wouldn't have been ruined by Niu Heifeng." Liang Xiaoyun clicked her tongue at the side of her cherry lips and said with contempt, "Look how anxious you are. How unpromising. I say, you big bookworm, please be quiet and listen to me explain and enlighten you. Is that okay?" An Yutian answered with a long face, "Okay. Please tell me." Liang Xiaoyun smiled and said, "Don't you know that everyone who is doing errands now is winning the world with empty talk? As long as you can fool Lao Ye into believing you and trick him into writing his name on the commission, you can naturally boast and rally many people. Those bandits and militias, who doesn't have a craving for officialdom? Who doesn't want to dabble in a formal change of name? As long as you spread the word, you won't have to worry about those people coming to you to solicit business. Then you show some discernment and use some tricks to select a few people who really have some power and give them a name that can rally people. Appoint them as chiefs and battalion commanders, and maintain good connections with them so that they are willing to support you and benefit themselves after success. That's like gathering wood to make a forest and gathering fur to make a robe. They will go down one level at a time to find people. Then, when you add them all up to make a whole number, it won't be so difficult. Even if you can't gather a full number at that time, rely on having a small foundation and try to say some nice things to Lao Ye, asking him to allocate some more military equipment and allow you to recruit some new soldiers as supplements. Eventually, you can turn the fake into the real and completely organize the new troops. If you don't first fool him with these dazzling words, and honestly say that you want to start a new stove and establish a new army, or ask him to allocate an existing team to you, firstly, his troops have long become the private property of his senior officers. No one will let you interfere. Of course, he can't allocate them. Secondly, he, as a high-ranking official, is most afraid of trouble. He knows that it takes a lot of money and equipment to establish a team out of thin air. How could he just give you so much money? Then the conversation will be unpleasant. Don't expect him to agree to such a big topic. This will be like you said, you can only do a nominal errand and never climb to a high branch."

Silk and Tea in Jiangyin: Changes in Spring Silkworm Rearing

Continuous Thunderstorms and Hail... Silkworms and Mulberry Trees Suffer Damage

In the four rural districts of Jiangyin, this year, fewer than half as many farmers are raising silkworms compared to last year. After the silkworm eggs hatched, there were continuous days of rain, sudden cold snaps, and sudden heat waves, causing the silkworms to develop sluggishly. Early silkworms only reached the stage of the first sleep before consuming leaves, while late silkworms only reached the second sleep. Recently, there was a heavy thunderstorm followed by hail, causing the silkworms to mutate and change. They spit out foul water, their bodies turned black, their abdomens ruptured and rotted, and the stench spread rapidly. The mulberry trees also suffered damage, with the price of leaves rising to eight to ten yuan per picul.

Listless Silk Market in Foreign Concessions

Yesterday, the silk market in the foreign concessions remained listless. Although reports were received from New York and Lyon via telegram, the prices offered were still low. Considering the cost of the factories and the loan requirements, each bale still incurred a loss of over two hundred taels. There were no transactions reported. Soon, new silk will be on the market. If the price of silk in Europe and America does not rise, the prospects for the silk market are viewed with increasing pessimism.

Hongcha from the River Port Opens for Trading

Yesterday, in the tea market in the foreign concessions, the Hongcha from the River Port [Hekou] of Jiangxi Province was opened for trading by Jardine Matheson at a price of fifty-five taels, which is twenty-five taels lower than last year. Due to a loosening of market conditions and a continued decline in the price of silver, the various firms trading in Hongcha from Qimen and Fuliang were showing strong interest. Total transactions for the city reached over two thousand three hundred taels, with prices ranging from ninety to one hundred and sixty-five taels, which is twenty chests lower than before. As for the green tea market, needle-shaped [Zhen] and eyebrow-shaped [Xiu Mei] teas are selling well, while precious eyebrow [Zhen Mei] teas have become sluggish. No further offerings have been seen from the Tunxi region or from the plucked bud [chouxin] variety.

Grain and Rice Market: Scarce and Selling Well

South Shanghai: Yesterday, few ships arrived from the interior, and the stocks at the docks were not abundant. Trading in the street became increasingly active. The price of fresh Northern Japonica rice and Zhongguan rice rose by one or two jiao compared to before. There was a shortage of thin paddy rice, and the opening price was fixed. There was a scarcity of superior reed paddy rice [Lu Yang Jian Huo], and the price remained unchanged. Early rice, white rice, and Flying Phoenix rice were sold as soon as they arrived, and the price rose by a few jiao. Tongbian Yin Yuan wine dealers continued to handle nearly a thousand piculs, with the opening price fluctuating by one or two jiao. Due to flooding on the Yangtze River, foreign rice was still being shipped to customers, and the market rebounded.

North Shanghai: The weather cleared up, and the sources from various groups were from the Nianliuqihao [perhaps a location]. Because the Dragon Boat Festival is approaching, the shops were unwilling to add more stock, and the prices of various goods gradually rose. There was a limited supply of Qingjiao Fenglian thin paddy rice, and the price was firm by a few jiao. Changshu Northern Japonica rice also rose by two jiao. Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

The Recent Impeachment Case

— Guliang

Regarding the case of the President of the Control Yuan, Yu Youren, impeaching the President of the Executive Yuan, Wang Jingwei, yesterday I read a Nanjing dispatch in this newspaper stating: "The Central Supervisory Committee resolved that the case of Yu Youren impeaching Wang Zhaoming should not be discussed further, taking a passive attitude. On the 24th, Yu submitted his resignation to the Central Executive Committee. Wang also felt deeply uneasy and submitted his resignation as well. On the afternoon of the 24th, the Central Standing Committee held a special discussion, and everyone agreed that the Control Yuan is responsible for investigating and impeaching, and that it showed the independent spirit of the Five Yuan by exercising its powers without avoiding suspicion or resentment. The Executive Yuan submitted the armistice agreement after it had been passed by the Central Political Council, which was also in order. It was unanimously decided to sincerely retain both presidents Yu and Wang."

One is seeking to resign because the impeachment was ineffective, and the other is resigning because he feels uneasy! But the Central Standing Committee is using "deeply demonstrated the independent spirit of the Five Yuan" and "also in order" to separately retain them. Who is legal and who is illegal, is not mentioned.

But from "exercising its powers without avoiding suspicion or resentment, deeply demonstrated...!" we can see that the impeachment was correct, and the impeached party should be punished! If we argue from "passed by the Central Political Council, which was also in order," then it seems that the Control Yuan's impeachment was improper and close to slander.

In any case, I believe that one of the two sides is wrong. This concerns the national legislation and cannot be glossed over. Is it "illegal"? Or is it "slanderous impeachment"? The truth should be clarified. If it is buried without resolution, it would be unfair and without principles.

Literature and Art

Banquet for Teacher Tang Weizhi, Two Quatrains

— Mengtiaoyan Master

Teacher Tang Weizhi came to Shanghai to avoid the war, and had a public banquet with fellow students.

After the war, the virtuous still gather, not many tears are shed at the new pavilion. In front of the wine, a song about the destruction of the homeland, the alligator is angry, the dragon is worried, unbearable to hear.

Hundreds of millions of feelings enter mournful chants, tribulations are hard to erase, the heart chases the sun. White hair relives the Tianbao dream, a testament written with deep wine stains. (Teacher was robbed on the way to Shanghai but escaped).

Feeling After Long Overcast Skies in Shanghai

— Ding Songzhai

Miserable mist and sorrowful clouds cannot be unlocked, the heart of heaven is silent and full of grief. As if pitying the wronged souls after the war, rain sprinkles like tears of people.

Science

Candle Manufacturing Method (II)

— Yun Li

(III) Manufacturing Procedures

First, use a soft cloth dampened with a little kerosene to coat the inside and outside of the candle-making machine cylinder once. Then use a clean cloth to wipe dry to remove dust. Then, insert the wick into the mold hole and fix it on the machine. Next, put the prepared raw materials into a pot to melt. After the oil is completely melted, remove the fire under the pot and wait for a moment for the temperature to decrease before pouring it into the mold. Then, run cold water outside the mold to allow the candle to solidify completely. Then, take it out and cut the end of the candle with a knife to make an ordinary candle.

(IV) Candle Coloring Method

First, put a little stearin into a pot and heat it until it melts. Then, grind the required pigment into a fine powder and put it into the stearin to mix and melt. Then, add this mixed pigment to a solution of paraffin and stearin, and stir vigorously to make the color uniform. Then, follow the procedure for making ordinary candles, pour it into the machine cylinder, and you're done.

(V) Candle Packaging Method

After the candles are made, they must be wrapped in paper, with each package containing six or twelve candles. This is determined by the convenience of each manufacturer. The outer layer of the wrapping paper is usually made of blue, hard cardboard, and the inner layer is sandwiched with a white waxed paper.

(VI) Mold Purchase

The best molds for making candles are made of galvanized iron, because galvanized iron does not produce brown rust. Copper molds should not be used, because copper easily produces green rust, which cannot produce clean white candles. The value of the machine depends on the size of the candle being made. Large ones cost about several tens of yuan, while small ones only cost six or seven to ten yuan. The ones sold by Mobil Oil Company are the best.

A Corner of Society

Lane Education

— Wuwei

| Miscellaneous Thoughts II |

In Shanghai, where land is at a premium, the courtyard of a house is only as big as a square table, which aptly matches the name "well". The front building, back building, side rooms, and pavilion rooms of a house are inhabited by no fewer than five or six families. To take a breath of fresh air, one has to go to the lane. Especially for playful children, the lane becomes their public entertainment ground.

In every lane, you can encounter more than five kinds of food vendors and more than ten kinds of people, each doing their different work in their own society.

I am fortunate to be born in this metropolis, and even more fortunate to live in the most complex corner of this metropolis 丨 Zhabei. Around me, I am surrounded by the noise of factories and workers. When I am writing, I often stick my head out the window to get some fresh air. Therefore, the activities in the lane often come into my eyes and cause a kind of unwarranted emotion.

The people active in this small world are mostly children from Jiangbei. "'Dahua Evening News! Do you want the Dahua Evening News!' A child is holding a piece of paper and walking around there, imitating the tone of a newspaper seller.

Come on! I'm not afraid of you! Several children are holding bamboo poles and fighting there. The more timid ones are cheering from behind, or scolding. Several more are practicing their skills under the wall, supporting themselves on the ground with both hands, their feet facing the sky, turning their bodies upside down. A smaller one tries to do the same, but his hands slip, and his head hits the cement floor with a thud and he cries. 'Useless fellow! Crying is not a good skill!' The people next door say with contempt. Then another one stands upside down. Another group is rolling coins.

'Dang! Got it, now you owe me five!' the winner says. Another group is now putting on a symbolic cast drama. A child is riding on another child's back, patting and walking, as if riding a horse. At the entrance of the lane, there is a candy vendor using the sound of a lottery stick tube to attract children's money. In addition to getting candy, the children also learn gambling skills. In their small minds, they will cleverly apply it to other things, guessing how many copper coins or beans are held in the hand! They can also bet on who will win. In this small society, they learn as much as possible the lessons given to them by the environment, and they also learn words that are enough to insult the other party and make them angry 丨 this is their education. They live in this environment from morning to night, just waiting, waiting for the old man to send them to the factory.

Alas! Poor factory candidates, this is what I think every time I see them.

The Question of Sex

Transformation

She is an elementary school teacher at my school. The students secretly call her Aunt Wang. Originally, she was extremely quiet, did not like to talk and laugh, and even less liked to powder her face and perm her hair. In particular, she extremely disliked watching movies.

Several days ago, through the introduction of her friend Ms. Ling, she was introduced to a boyfriend, Mr. B. He was a classmate of Ms. Ling's brother and was studying at a certain university. Since the two of them met, her attitude has changed greatly. Her face is painted like a big A Fu doll bought from Wuxi, and she often has two blood-red lips, chatting and laughing with her colleagues. Her former quiet attitude has been invisibly eliminated. Her hair is curly, like the barbed wire fence during martial law. She has really changed, completely changed.

One day, Hui told me that she had seen Aunt Wang watching a movie with B at the Beijing Theater. At first, I didn't believe it. Later, I often heard students say that they met her with B at the Carlton watching a movie, and another day they saw her at the Gan Theater watching a movie with B.

One Sunday afternoon, Hui and Ling came to my house and asked me to go to the French Park to play. At that time, I was sitting at home and really felt bored, and it had been a long time since I had been to the park to play, so I immediately went with them. But things coincided extremely well. The three of us were sitting on a bench under a big tree talking when he and B happened to come side by side. He didn't recognize us, so he still raised his head and puffed out his chest, walking proudly. But she had already seen us. She felt a little embarrassed, lowered her head, turned red, and pretended not to see us, going around another path. This time I finally felt that my trip was worthwhile, seeing a scene of a live love play.

It was such an unexpected turn of events. One day, after finishing night school, we were all reading in the dormitory when Hui ran into the dormitory, jumping and skipping, and said softly; "Hey! Do you know that Aunt Wang has lost her love? Her boyfriend has changed his mind. I heard that he already has another very beautiful girlfriend."

"How would you know? I don't think so," I said to Hui in surprise.

"Who's kidding you, everyone knows it, and someone has already seen B watching a movie with that girl at a certain big theater. Their attitude was very intimate," Hui said boastfully.

"Then does Aunt Wang know?" I couldn't help asking her.

"Of course she knows, that's why she hasn't been to school for two days," Hui said.

"Oh, no wonder, I haven't seen him for two days," Shan said quietly.

"Alas: I really don't know, they were so intimate, how could it come to this," Zhu said.

"These kinds of people are worthy of having received such a high education," I said angrily in silence.

"Oh! A man's heart is really unpredictable," Shan said, shaking her head.

The dinner bell rang in the midst of the chaotic noise, interrupting our conversation.

School Writing

Mr. and Miss

— Yingdai

Mr. is a pronoun for gentleman, and Miss is a pronoun for young lady. Although these two nouns are borrowed from the English dictionary, they are spoken very naturally in the mouths of Chinese people. If you don't believe me, look at the first sentence that modern young men and fashionable young women say when they meet, it is always Mr. X and Miss X.

The principal of C School is an American student. Because he has been abroad, he has brought back a lot of foreign airs. He usually refers to teachers and students as Mr. or Miss, which is so polite and so equal.

The principal is so polite to the students, so the other teachers certainly don't dare to put on airs and show their dignity. Therefore, every time the roll is called, the names of the male students are added with Mr., and the names of the female students are added with Miss.

One day, a substitute teacher came. He also knew the school spirit of C School, but when he got a roll book, he couldn't tell who was Mr. and who was Miss in a classroom where boys and girls were sitting together. After hesitating for a while, he finally came up with a way.

His method was to look at the names on the roll book and add Mr. to the male names and Miss to the female names. Because most Chinese names can be used to distinguish between men and women at a glance, but even if he guessed some of them correctly, some girls might have male names, and some boys might have female names. A joke therefore occurred.

Boys were added with Miss, and girls were added with Mr. After discovering the mistake once, there was a burst of laughter in the classroom. By the time he finished calling the roll, all the students in the class were laughing so hard that they couldn't catch their breath.

A Female Student's Leather Satchel

— Changmu

It was almost noon, twelve o'clock, and everyone's stomachs were rumbling, hoping to be dismissed from class quickly, but the dismissal bell hadn't rung yet. The teacher was standing on the podium, pointing and drawing and talking non-stop.

Clang! The bell only rang once, without waiting for the teacher to say "dismissed," everyone grabbed their books, stood up, and ran outside.

The very narrow classroom door was blocked by many people, surging forward and pushing backward, all wanting to return home as quickly as possible, their hearts like those of criminals being released from prison.

Clang!

The sound of something falling to the ground. Everyone's gaze focused on the source of the sound. Suddenly, a burst of intoxicating fragrance touched everyone's sense of smell.

A female student bent down and picked up what had fallen on the ground and put it into her small and exquisite leather satchel. In addition to a few textbooks and lecture notes, others discovered that in that female student's leather satchel, there was also a bottle of "Three Flowers Brand Snow Cream," a box of "Kou Dan," and a tube of "Kiss Proof." Unfortunately, a bottle of Cappl perfume had already been broken on the ground.

This is a question, what did that female student bring those things to school for? Could it be that there is a "beauty practice" subject in the school?

Page 14

!

Chain Education Yunguang

One Saturday at noon, Mr. Sun was supposed to accompany his wife to the movies as usual. But because yesterday in the writing room, his colleague Lao Wang talked about how fun roulette was, which Mr. Sun listened to with great interest, so he was moved. He and Lao Wang agreed to go to the roulette gambling place to play together today, so he had to take leave from his wife for the movie class. And afraid that his wife would be lonely at home, he took out twenty yuan in banknotes and gave it to his wife, asking her to invite a few little sisters next door to play mahjong to relieve boredom. Mrs. Sun took the banknotes and no longer asked Mr. Sun to accompany her to the movies. Mr. Sun walked out of his door, secretly pleased, "This kind of woman is really annoying, she wants to go out together at every turn, today I'm relieved."

An hour later, Mr. Sun was placing bets in the roulette gambling place, and Mrs. Sun was inviting little sisters to play cards at home.

Mrs. Sun's son, Baoguan, was only nine years old. When he came back from school, he saw his mother, grabbed the corner of her clothes, and tore and缠缠 [Chanchan - cling], wanting his mother to accompany him to buy stone pencils and rubber balls. Mrs. Sun couldn't work because Baoguan was making a fuss, so she took out a handful of copper coins from beside her and gave them to Baoguan, telling him to go to the candy stall at the entrance of the alley to bet on candy to eat.

Baoguan got the money and no longer made a fuss. He went happily to bet on candy. When Mrs. Sun was playing cards, she felt relieved without Baoguan tearing and缠缠 beside her.

From then on, as soon as Mr. Sun left the writing room, he went to the roulette gambling place to place bets. As soon as Mrs. Sun got home, she invited little sisters to play cards to relieve boredom. As soon as Baoguan came back from school, he went to the entrance of the alley to bet on candy, developing a family habit of gambling.

Some say that Baoguan's liking for betting on candy was developed by Mrs. Sun. Mrs. Sun's liking for playing cards was developed by Mr. Sun. Mr. Sun's liking for roulette was developed by Lao Wang. Who developed Lao Wang's liking for roulette, I don't know.

Art End

Mending-Poor Women Rope Wu

No matter which lane or which road, in the morning or afternoon, there are often mending-poor women carrying ingot baskets coming and going, which is convenient for pedestrians. They neither shout loudly nor hoard goods to sell at a high price. They assess how life is, how much to charge for mending, and make a decisive decision without delay. We, the out-of-towners without family members, when our clothes are torn, we call them to mend them, when our socks are broken, we call them to darn them. Throughout the year, we invisibly get a lot of convenience and endless practical benefits. We should thank them deeply.

Why are they called mending-poor? Is it because they are poor and mend for others, so they are called mending-poor, or is it because they specialize in mending for poor people, so they are called mending-poor? I have asked many people, but there has not been even half a definitive answer. It is still a question.

Don't their ingot baskets each contain a pair of small stools? I once heard someone say, "If their stools have their four legs facing the sky, then they have another lover who is in a similar profession (shoemaker) in addition to their legally recognized husband." But I have carefully watched and never seen any stools facing the sky. Could it be that all mending-poor women are of bad character? I think the person who said this was probably deliberately trying to damage their reputation.

Let's not worry about their character. In short, they are beneficial to us drifters, so we should thank them and respect them.

Necessary

The Pursuit of Wildflowers

Flood

This is truly a one-act play about the future of China that I personally overheard in Zhaofeng Park.

One person, Yu Shihe, said, "As soon as we entered the park gate, the sun was extraordinarily bright, and the sky was extraordinarily blue and green!" A tall young man in a well-tailored Western suit said as he walked alongside a short, stout young man also in Western suit and leather shoes. "That's not necessarily true; it's more like breathing in the clean, fresh air is as refreshing as kissing a young woman."

"Exactly! This alone is worth the price of our 'skipping class'! Moreover..." He then raised a kind of "walking stick" used as an accessory, pointing it remotely towards the willow shade deep in the moving place, painted a semicircle and then said: "These beautiful and inexhaustible blessings are preparing for us to appreciate at will, just like opening an exhibition!"

"Who cares! No matter what, it can't compare to those 'all modern' female classmates in the 'Gathering of Heroes Studio' on the floor opposite our dormitory; it's a pity that the school has moved now, making one feel the 'carved railings and jade stairs should still be there, but the rosy faces have changed.'"

"Speaking of the closest vantage points in school, what about the Bai sisters in my class? But I always find them 'not as fragrant as wildflowers'!"

"Old Wang! I don't know how many thousands of times I've heard the famous Bai sisters in your mouth, but in reality, I'm afraid even their farts are hard to smell!"

"Old Wang! Don't overestimate the female students,"

"They also like to joke around with us! For example, in today's physics and chemistry class, because the noise from the second row of students was a bit loud, they made 'Shh...' sounds of scolding, but fortunately, a classmate shouted out a funny remark, 'Quick, bring a chamber pot, be careful the spring water leaks into the lecture hall,' which suppressed them with their faces flushed red."

"Ha... It's amazing that he could come up with such a surprising and effective joke on the spur of the moment, what a genius!"

"Heck! The day before yesterday, I even had a kind of relationship with them personally. When I was engrossed in reading Dream of the Red Chamber, suddenly a sound of scolding like an oriole complaining and a swallow getting angry, 'A good dog doesn't block the road,' gently entered my eardrums. Looking back, it turned out that the Bai sisters were standing gracefully..." Saying this, he actually supplemented it with a "looking back" pose and discovered a person wearing rubber-soled shoes (not the Bai sisters, but actually me) was closely following them listening in on their conversation, so he acted surprised, "changed the subject," and of course, I had to be sensible and slink off onto the grass. What kind of tricks this unfinished drama will perform later, there is no way to find out!

Movies

Iron Evidence Re-Releases Soon the blood case film Iron Evidence of a profligate woman, (The Silent Witness), which was once screened at the Nanjing Grand Theatre, stars Adhui. Adhui, with his genius for drama, stars in the film. The pinnacle of art and the deep impression of the performance on the hearts of people have long been admired by the ladies of Shanghai. It is a rare masterpiece. Now, the theater, in response to the enthusiastic demands of all walks of life, will re-screen the film on Friday and Saturday for two days to comfort those who have not seen this film and alleviate their desire to view it. It is said that the film will soon leave the port, so those who want to see it must not miss this good opportunity.

Four Horsemen to Be Released Tomorrow The Carlton Theatre will release the war epic Four Horsemen tomorrow (Friday). The war epic "All Quiet on the Western Front," which has shaken the world, has already won excellent reputation in the past. However, the film "Four Horsemen" is an unprecedented epic film made by the German film industry with all its strength to counter "All Quiet on the Western Front." Its depiction of war is more realistic than "All Quiet on the Western Front," and the spirit of soldiers who are unyielding and willing to sacrifice their lives for their country is even more admirable.

Historical War Masterpiece Lincoln The historical war masterpiece Lincoln is a masterpiece directed by master director Griffith and was selected as the second of the top ten films of 1931. Its intense plot, passionate performance, magnificent scenery, realistic battlefield, tragic military music, and noble purpose are unmatched by other films. When watching the exciting parts, people are inspired with loyalty and courage. The sad parts make people linger and want to die. It expresses infinite sympathy for this generation of great men and is a rare and excellent film. It will be released at the Paris Grand Theatre starting today. There are not many good seats, so please come early.

Huang Xiaochi Gives Away All His Flowers The calligrapher and painter Huang Xiaochi is famous for his landscapes and figures. Each foot costs only one yuan for ink fees. For example, if you buy a four-foot screen, it only costs eight yuan (five feet cost ten yuan) and you get a free couplet. Mail address: No. 5, Xinxing Shunli, Ganshi East Road, French Concession, Shanghai, and various fan shops.

Kemei Obstetrics Hospital Adds a Branch The Kemei Obstetrics Hospital, behind the Sincere Company in this city, originally had two branches in Hongkou and the French Concession. The Hongkou branch was closed due to the war. Now, because residents in the Hongkou area have moved back and there are more births, they have found No. 161 Tangshan Road and opened the Hongkou branch to facilitate childbirth nearby.

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court

Criminal Judgment Liu Shiding is sentenced to 20 days of detention for each of the two counts of theft, for a total of 30 days of detention. ▲ Jin Amao is sentenced to two years of imprisonment for the crime of habitual theft. Zhu Zhenfu is fined 20 yuan for the crime of knowingly buying stolen goods. ▲ Zhuang Jujin is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined eighty yuan for intending to make a profit by providing a house for others to smoke opium substitutes. Li Fusheng is sentenced to three months of imprisonment and fined thirty yuan for helping to intend to make a profit by providing a house for others to smoke opium substitutes. Yang Huiqing, Zhang Lanqing, Yan Boan, and Qiu Geshi are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined ten yuan for smoking opium substitutes. Jiang Zhixiang, i.e., Jiang Zixiang, is sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for smoking opium as a repeat offender. Zhang Lanqing and Qiu Geshi are granted a two-year reprieve. Cao A Gen and Yang Genshou are both not guilty. Wang Dejin is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing a house for others to smoke opium. Chen Rongsheng, Li Yongxiang, and Yang Suibai are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium. Li Yongxiang is granted a two-year reprieve. ▲ Xu Jinhe is fined 40 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. ▲ Wang Ada is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing a house for others to smoke opium substitutes. Yang Cailang, Xu Fucai, Zhao Laoda, Yao Jinchen, and Xu Bingpu are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. ▲ Chen Weikui is fined 50 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. ▲ Li Yueyao is fined 40 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. ▲ Gao Zhengsheng is fined 30 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. ▲ Feng Huchen is fined 15 yuan for possessing opium substitutes. ▲ Lu Shengfu is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined eighty yuan for intending to make a profit by providing a house for others to smoke opium substitutes. Zhang Zhaoshi is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for helping to intend to make a profit by providing a house for others to smoke opium substitutes. Xu Gensheng, Shao Junyang, Guo A'er, Xu Gensheng, Ye Jiaxing, Zhu Shilin, and Hua Renyuan are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined ten yuan for smoking opium substitutes. Zhang Zhaoshi, Ye Jia, Xu Genshan, and Hua Renyuan are granted a two-year reprieve. ▲ Zhu Jinsheng is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined ten yuan for intending to make a profit by providing a house for others to smoke opium. Gu Yaoting is granted a two-year reprieve. ▲ Zhu A Jin is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined thirty yuan for intending to make a profit by providing a house for others to smoke opium substitutes. Chen Hanzhang and Zhu Daxin are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined ten yuan for smoking opium. Miao Ada is sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined five yuan for attempting to smoke opium substitutes. Zhu A Jin and Miao Ada are granted a three-year reprieve. ▲ Wang Chenshi is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined three hundred yuan for intending to make a profit by providing a house for others to smoke opium. Chen Renting is sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined fifty yuan for smoking opium, with a three-year reprieve. ▲ Xu Xianzhang is sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment and fined three thousand six hundred yuan for manufacturing opium substitutes. Lu Chengxiang is not guilty. ▲ Yu Amao is fined 30 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. ▲ Zheng A'er is fined 40 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. ▲ Weng Xinwu is fined 30 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. ▲ Zhang Fushan is fined 50 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. ▲ Zhang Shirong and Zhou Jinshan are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. ▲ Yang Zhengyuan is fined 60 yuan for possessing opium substitutes. ▲ Sun Mashi is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. Liu Zhiwen is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes, with a three-year reprieve. ▲ Xu A Qing is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined sixty yuan for intending to make a profit by providing a house for others to smoke opium substitutes. Wang Xiuying is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for attempting to smoke opium, with a three-year reprieve (May 25).

Shanghai Local Court

Civil Judgment Wu Qiheng v. Zhang Ziheng for fraud with incidental civil suit. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,400 yuan in silver and interest at a rate of 1.2% per month from January 1, 1931, until the end of the execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhang Yishi v. Zhang Zhangfu for divorce. The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. ▲ Xu Haiming et al. v. Ling Shunmei for execution objection. The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. ▲ Feng Langzhai v. Li Fumei for divorce. The marriage between the plaintiff and the defendant is approved for divorce. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.
